### Post by justbick on 2013-10-29
Recently I upgraded from 13.04, where scroll down worked fine. Now when you hold middle button in down position on touchpad it only move roughly one line whereas it would have moved down the page. Any ideas? I plugged in a usb mouse and everything worked ok..
